\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Valid for the naturals, but what if \isa{{\isadigit{0}}\ {\isacharless}{\kern0pt}\ i\ {\isacharless}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}}? Premises cannot be
  weakened: consider the case where \isa{i\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{0}}}, \isa{m\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}} and \isa{n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{0}}}.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
